***рыбина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыбина.html>ры́бина</a> (16692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rýba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбина.html>ры́бина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýbina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбина.html>ры́бины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбина.html>ры́бины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбина.html>ры́бин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> big fish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ribband, diagonal; batten</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýbnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:садок.html>садо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnyj</b> sadók</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fish</b> pond</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:суп.html>суп</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnyj</b> sup</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fish</b> soup</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рынок.html>ры́нок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnyj</b> rýnok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fish</b> market</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:торговля.html>торго́вля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnaja</b> torgóvlja</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fish</b> trade</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:промышленность.html>промы́шленность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnaja</b> promýšlennostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fishing</b> industry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловля.html>ло́вля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnaja</b> lóvlja</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fish</b>ing</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>fish</b> catching</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnyj</b> prómysel</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fish</b>ery</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:консервы.html>консе́рвы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnyje</b> konsérvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">canned <b>fish</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>fish</b> canned goods</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>abounding in fish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>река́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýbnaja</b> reká</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">river <b>abounding in fish</b>; <b>fish-filled</b> river</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ры<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́ц<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыдание.html>рыда́ние</a> (9770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыдать.html>рыда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rydátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыдание.html>рыда́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rydánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыдание.html>рыда́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыдание.html>рыда́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыдание.html>рыда́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sobbing, weeping</li></ol>

***рыдать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыдать.html>рыда́ть</a> (5339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рыдати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rydati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rydati</i>.

<p><b>ры́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жий</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a/c. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>рыже́е</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>рыже́й</a>, порыже́е, порыже́й.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рыж-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:морковный.html>морко́вный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:медный.html>ме́дный</a></li>

<p><b>ры́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жий</b>

Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рык.html>рык</a> (9734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рык.html>рык</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ryk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рык.html>ры́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рык.html>ры́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рык.html>ры́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>roar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:львиный.html>льви́ный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рык.html>рык</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lʹvínyj ryk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lion's roaring</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***рыло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́ло</a> (6943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rylo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rydlo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spade, snout</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýlo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́л</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыльце.html>ры́льце</a></b>)

***рында.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нда</a> (30576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýnda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an armor-bearer or bodyguard of a Muscovite tsar</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">armor-bearer</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оруженосец.html>оружено́сец</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oruženósec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bodyguard</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:телохранитель.html>телохрани́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">teloxranítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a mondegreen of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">“ring the bell”</i>, a British officer's command interpreted as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">«<a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бей</a>»</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">“rýndu bej”</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strike the rynda</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> by Russian sailors.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýnda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рында.html>ры́нд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> three triple strikes of a ship's bell marking noon in Russian naval tradition</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a ship's bell</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">ship's bell</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судовой.html>судово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колокол.html>ко́локол</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sudovój kólokol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колокол.html>ко́локол</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">korabélʹnyj kólokol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ры́н<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ры́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нок</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***рыскать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыскать.html>ры́скать</a> (11334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рыскати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ryskati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto-Slavic root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*risk-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыскать.html>ры́скать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýskatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to prowl, to scour <i>(about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыскать.html>ры́скать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>берегу</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лесу</a>]</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýskatʹ</b> po beregu [lesu]</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scour the coast [woods]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rummage <i>(in)</i>, to ransack
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыскать.html>ры́скать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rýskatʹ</b> glazámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rove</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gripe, to yaw</li></ol>

***рысь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рысь.html>рысь</a> (13494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rysь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewk-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lynx</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рытвина.html>ры́твина</a> (17865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рытва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rytva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>рыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рытвина.html>ры́твина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýtvina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рытвина.html>ры́твины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рытвина.html>ры́твины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рытвина.html>ры́твин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pothole</li>
<li>pit</li></ol>

***рыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>рыть</a> (7258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ryti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rūti</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(H)RewH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>рыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырыть.html>вы́рыть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нары́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подры́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dig</li>
<li>to burrow, to mine</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копать.html>копа́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>ры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***рыцарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́царь</a> (2571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rycerz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ritter</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ritter</i>. The form is influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́царь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýcarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́царя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́цари</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́царей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>knight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́ть</a> (кого́-либо) <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́цари</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posvjaščátʹ (kovó-libo) v <b>rýcari</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knight (someone)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:странствующий.html>стра́нствующий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыцарь.html>ры́царь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stránstvujuščij <b>rýcarʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">knight-errant</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***рычать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рычать.html>рыча́ть</a> (6638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рычать.html>рыча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ryčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прорычать.html>прорыча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grumble, to growl, to snarl <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a low growling or rumbling animal noise</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
